20/04/23, 8:05â€¯am -  CR1: Please find below email received from Bureau of Indian Standards (BIS) regarding requirement of interns.  

Eligibility: Students pursuing Under graduation (B.Tech. passing out Batch 2023 and 2024) or Post-Graduation (M.Tech. & Ph.D., having completed studies of at least 2 Semesters). 

The students must have minimum 75% Marks or Cumulative Grade Point Average (CGPA) of 7.5 out of 10 as on the last semester, whose result has been declared.

Internship Duration: 2 months (check point No. 5 in the email).

Other details are provided in the email. 

HOD's / Placement-in-Charge's are requested to send the duly filled proforma (soft copy pdf) for all the interested candidates.

Last Date to send the applications : 21 April, 2023, 12.00 noon
20/04/23, 8:05â€¯am -  CR1: Dear Madam/Sir,
 
As you may be aware, Bureau of Indian Standards (BIS) is the National Standards Body of India, established under an Act of Parliament, the BIS Act, 2016. It is engaged in the activities of Standardization at national & international levels and operating Conformity Assessment Schemes such as the Product Certification Scheme (popularly known as the ISI Marking Scheme), Hallmarking of Gold & Silver articles and Management System Certification etc. All these activities are aimed at creating a vibrant quality ecosystem in the country to ensure availability of quality goods & services to the consumers through the industries implementing the quality standards.
 
2. BIS intends to engage students as interns for conducting Pre-Standardization study under the technical deptts. of BIS at Delhi. The internship programme includes the following:
 
a.  Orientation programme at National Institute of Training for standardization (NITS), Noida â€“ the training wing of BIS.
b.  Finalization of topic of study in consultation with HoD and Member secretary of the technical deptt.
c.  Examination of existing technical literature, survey, including journals, articles, research reports, and related national / international reports if any.
d.  Horizon scanning of the entire quality ecosystem for identification of key stakeholders like leading manufacturers (both large and small scale covering the entire spectrum of industry), organized users and target groups, testing laboratories, R&D institutions etc.
e.  Interaction with stakeholders including visit to manufacturers / labs and stakeholdersâ€™ meetings.
f.   Analysis of manufacturing processes from sustainability angle.
g.  Pre-submission consultation with technical deptt and member secretary.
h.  Preparation of draft specification.
 
3. The interns will be paid a monthly stipend of Rs. 20,000/-.
 
4. The students will be benefitted from this exercise in terms of not only getting a sound understanding of the importance and status of standards and quality consciousness in diverse sectors of Indian economy but also gain an insight into the process of standardization, implementation of standards and the role of India in International standardization. This will, in addition, help them to hone their skills for empirical study and research-related work.
 
5. As for the Structure of the Internship Programme, it will be mandatory for the interns to work for a fortnight, under the direct supervision of the Standardization Department concerned. The concerned department may allow the interns to work from home thereafter. However, the intern shall be in constant touch with the Standardization Department and must attend VCs or webinars organized by BIS to discuss their work. Draft report should be submitted positively between the 40th & the 45th day of the assignment and the final report, within the 55th day, incorporating the suggestions and comments on the draft report, and subsequent presentation will follow thereafter until the end of internship.
 
6. It is requested to send the nominations for the interns as per the Following Annexures and Proformas (enclosed herein). The proformas have to be filled and signed by the Student/ Institute as mentioned:
a) Application proforma (As per Annex II) by each candidate;
b) Acceptance of Terms and Conditions of Internship (Appendix A of Annex II) by each candidate;
c) Undertaking by the Institute/University (Page 2 of Annex II) for each of the candidates;

 

Regards,

03/04/24, 10:09â€¯am - Student P: *Actual Arguments:*
The arguments listed in the function calling statement are referred to as actual arguments. They are the actual values passed to a function to compute a value or to perform a task.
03/04/24, 10:09â€¯am - Student P: *Formal Arguments:*
These are the parameters that are specified in the function definition. They act as placeholders for the values that will be passed to the function when it is called. In other words, they are the names used in the function definition to represent the values that the actual arguments will provide.

20/08/24, 4:28â€¯pm -  CR1: TCS Confidential

Dear Professor

 

Greetings!


We are delighted to introduce the Tata Imagination Challenge, India's largest idea competition organized by the Tata Group. This exciting platform empowers undergraduate and postgraduate students across all disciplines and years of study to share their innovative ideas for shaping a better tomorrow.


Last year, the challenge attracted a phenomenal response with over 2.63 lakh students participating from 10,000+ campuses across 1,200+ Indian cities and towns.


Why Participate?

Exciting Prizes: The competition offers attractive cash prizes (INR 2 lakh each for 10 winners) and Tata brand vouchers.
Career Opportunities: Winners have the chance to secure interviews for the prestigious Tata Administrative Services (TAS) program, launching a bright future with the Tata Group.
Learn from Leaders: Finalists and winners receive mentorship from renowned Tata leaders, gaining invaluable insights into the corporate world.

Competition Format:

Round 1 | Online Quiz: This round assesses students' knowledge of the Tata universe, quantitative analysis, and logical thinking skills.
Round 2 | Gamified Assessments: This engaging round involves a series of game-based challenges to further evaluate students' potential.
Round 3 | Video Pitch: Shortlisted candidates submit a compelling video pitch showcasing their ideas for change.
Final Round | Live Pitching: The top 50 finalists present their ideas directly to senior Tata leaders in Mumbai.

We kindly request your esteemed institution's support in spreading awareness about this exciting opportunity among your students. 

 

Registration is now open and will close by 9 September 2024. Students can register for the Tata Imagination Challenge by clicking this link:

https://www.tata.com/careers/programs/tata-imagination-challenge?utm_referral&utm_medium=banner&utm_campaign=TCSNextStep

 

For any further inquiries, please direct students to contact tataimaginationchallenge@tata.com.

 

Looking forward to your institution's active participation in this prestigious event.

For Online Assessments :

College must ensure labs have the required logistics arrangement made at their end as below:

Operating system: Windows 8 or 10 only
Google Chrome browser: version 80 (upto 5 latest versions can be considered)

VPN/Proxy should be disabled

Specifically for communication assessment:

This initiative is a stipend-based internship, designed to provide participants with practical exposure while working alongside professionals at MeitY (Ministry of Electronics and Information Technology) institutes. Work-Base Learning (WBL) programme (internship) brings an opportunity to acquire direct practical experience and exposure to the latest Information Technology, Electronics, and related areas. The Scheme is specifically devised for the Graduate Engineers of Scheduled Caste (SC), Scheduled Tribe (ST), Women, and Economically Weaker Section (EWS), keeping in view the social/economical background.

Objectives: 

Ã¼  It facilitates SC/ ST/ EWS/ Women candidates for transition from college environment to the corporate world, and thereby provides them with a real-time exposure on niche technological projects/ activity in organizations under MeitY.

Ã¼  The Programme provides direct practical experience and exposure to Fresh Graduates Engineers on Niche Technologies thereby reducing the â€œdeployable timeâ€ for both the candidate as well as the prospective employer.

Ã¼  It helps candidates attain stability between theoretical studies and realistic job exposure through hand-on expertise in Design/Developmental Skills, Requirement Analysis, Testing skills, Exposure to Standardization/QA etc.

Ã¼  Helps in enhancing professional skills among the candidates in various areas such as problem-solving abilities; communication skills; presentation skills, confidence enhancement, individual grooming, enterprise etiquettes, etc. 

About the Programme:
Duration: 6 months (Can be extended further 6 months based on the performance)
Categories Desired:  Scheduled Caste (SC), Scheduled Tribe (ST), Women, and Economically Weaker Section (EWS)
Eligibility: Last year students of B.Tech/B.E., M.Sc. & M.C.A or Last 3 year graduates in  B.Tech/B.E., M.Sc. & M.C.A.
Stipend: Rs. 10000 per month.

03/01/25, 4:25â€¯pm -  CR1: Subject: Joint â€œIndia Semiconductor Workforce Development Program (ISWDP)â€ | Cohort 4 Announcement and Samsung Fellowships

 

Dear Prof. 

 

Wishing you a Happy New Year! I hope this message finds you in good health and spirits. This is regarding the announcement of Cohort 4 of the India Semiconductor Workforce Development Program (ISWDP), run by the Indian Institute of Science (IISc) Bangalore, in collaboration with Synopsys Inc., USA, and Samsung Semiconductor India Research (SSIR). ISWDP is a program tailored to bridge the process technology and device design skill gap in the swiftly expanding semiconductor sector through a meticulously designed course, covering the foundational and advanced concepts, also offering a hands-on approach through microelectronics lab experience.

 

The live virtual program comprises four levels, i.e., Level 1, Level 2, Advance, and Custom. Launched in March 2024, the program runs 4 cohorts throughout the year. Following the successful completion of 3 cohorts with over 1500 participants, I am happy to announce that registrations are now open for Cohort 4, starting February 1, 2025 (view the schedule here). Cohort 4 of ISWDP introduces new developments and newer opportunities for students (such as Samsung-sponsored fellowships), and the programâ€™s further expansion (such as an expanded curriculum and industry-sponsored Custom Modules by Tektronix, Inc., and Rohde & Schwarz). More technical details of the program are available at: https://iisc-iswdp.org/pdf/iswdp.pdf

May we request your office to kindly disseminate this information to students and faculties of the concerned departments in your institute by forwarding this email and posting it on respective notice boards?   

 

How to enrol?

There are two ways for students to enrol for ISWDP:

Â·       Direct Registration: Students can simply click on this link for direct registration: https://iswdp.registeryourseat.in/index.php.

Â·       Samsung Fellowship: Alternatively, students can fill up the Google Form  https://forms.gle/o4G7sGwNA1uvzm3F7 by January 10th, 2025, to register through the Samsung Fellowship, more details of which can be found here https://iisc-iswdp.org/scholarship.php. Eligible students will be notified via email by January 20th, 2025.  We encourage meritorious students to register through this route.

 

Please note that the slots in each cohort are limited, so prompt action is advisable.

I hope your colleagues and students make the best use of this effort from IISc, Synopsys, and Samsung Semiconductor India Research. Please do not hesitate to reach out to me in case of questions. We will be regularly posting program schedules and other important updates on our LinkedIn page. Those interested in the program can follow us on LinkedIn at https://www.linkedin.com/company/iswdp/

 

PS: Institution Heads/ Dept. Heads/ Faculty can write to us at iswdp.msdlab@iisc.ac.in to learn more about the mode of engagement, modalities, and Return on Investment.

 

 

Best regards

India Semiconductor Workforce Development Program (ISWDP)
